                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1908">
                       Rustic Canyon is one of the most special, tucked away neighborhoods in all of Los Angeles. It is nestled among couple hundred ft tall trees, lush hills, and Rustic Creek, wedged between Santa Monica, Pacific Palisades, and the beach. It has some very famous architectural homes from the likes of Ray Kappe, Harwell Hamilton, Thornton Abell, Melinda Gray, David Hertz, etc, and is home to Hollywood celebs, famous artists, writers, producers, and other creative professionals. The entire neighborhood has a very casual, creative, comfortable feeling, despite many of the properties being in the $5-15 Million+ range.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1909">
                       <li data-reactid="1910"><p data-reactid="1911">Jason and Karen have been amazing hosts and their house, a serene, lush and quiet hide-away, has by far exceeded our expectations. From the beginning, Jason and his wife were perfect hosts - they even purchased a crib for our baby in advance and set up the place beautifully. The neighborhood is quiet, full of architectural homes and lush exotic trees - a true oasis in bustling LA and ideally located near the beach and palisades village. We had rented both the house and guest house in order to have maximum privacy, which was absolutely worth it. Due to the special microclimate of the area it never got too cold nor too hot and we had many occasions to use the large pool, jacuzzi, outdoor dining with BBQ. We were traveling as a family (parents, grandparents and baby) and for our needs, the house was perfect. It offers spacious bedrooms with great beds and baths, a large kitchen and living area that feels open and yet cozy, with all amenities that one might need (fast wifi , tv systems, books to read and so on). We will absolutely want to return and would recommend this place to everyone! </p><span data-reactid="1912">Viviana</span><span data-reactid="1913">2015-07-03T00:00:00Z</span></li>
